Special Report

An Appeal to the Nation Regarding the Japanese Disaster

(Ma Xiangbo, the "Old Man of Ninety-Two")

Correct Past Mistakes, Jointly Face the National Crisis

Redeem Ourselves, Save Ourselves, Revive the Nation

Today, the whole country mourns the Japanese disaster. Although I am old, I am also a citizen. Where duty calls, I cannot refuse. I express my views to encourage my fellow countrymen.

At this time of overlapping natural disasters, man-made calamities, external troubles, and internal strife, the people of the nation should understand that if a country is divided and cannot defend itself, it is because the country must first attack itself before others attack it. For the current situation, the best strategy is to redeem ourselves and save ourselves. Looking back at the current misfortunes, most of them are self-inflicted. Is it about money being exhausted? The money has been exhausted on military expenses of hundreds of millions of dollars, but there is no equipment for national defense. Is it about the people being impoverished? The people are impoverished, yet tens of millions of dollars are still spent on opium every year. However, no attention is paid to river defense. As a result, disasters suddenly erupt, and sixteen provinces become a marsh. The strong neighbor rejoices in our misfortune and launches a large-scale invasion. Thus, our territory and sovereignty outside Shanhaiguan have been completely trampled upon. The troubles of Lu have not ended; who is Qingfu? The people are not tired of chaos, so Heaven punishes China. Think about it quietly. Hubei attacks Hunan, and Guangxi attacks Guangdong. We are all from the same root; is there any gain or loss to be said? The cycle of civil war over the past twenty years is always the same. Alas! The country is poor and weak to this extreme. The government has no austerity measures, and the people have a penchant for extravagance. National morality is declining day by day, and the people's livelihood is becoming more and more difficult. Moreover, disaster is upon us. We recall the past glory of our history and the cultural heritage created by our ancestors. They gave us a great civilized country. Our future generations, even if they cannot promote and develop the ancestral legacy, should still follow in the footsteps of our ancestors and not fail to be a great nation. Only then can we be worthy of standing in the world. From now on, the people of the nation should have a clear resolve, correct past mistakes, redeem ourselves, save ourselves, unite our efforts, and jointly face the national crisis. Then, after ten years of recuperation and education, there will eventually be a day of self-strengthening and revival. Like the ancient sages Cheng Tang and Wei Wu, we should cultivate ourselves and take responsibility, which may help to turn the tide and save the nation. For without first restoring the inherent national moral spirit, there will be no truly loyal and willing citizens to sacrifice for the country. This can be stated with certainty. If the people have no sense of responsibility, then so be it. If they do, then please vow to start from today, redeem ourselves, save ourselves, and jointly face the national crisis. Moreover, since the Meiji Restoration, Japan's rapid progress in people's wisdom and morality has been impressive. This small island nation prides itself on being a great nation in East Asia. Its annexation and plundering have not been a matter of a day or two. It has been plotting to occupy our Northeast for nearly thirty years. Experts have designed and secretly implemented plans. But we are still fast asleep, allowing others to sleep soundly beside our bed. Only in the last two or three years have we begun to pay attention (such as establishing Japanese studies societies and other groups). They know us, but we do not know them. The battle is decided before it even begins. This time, the Japanese army's strong occupation of our famous cities in Liaoning and Jilin is like taking something out of a pocket. We have not resisted at all and have endured it. Is this not the same as waiting for death with our hands tied? Our land is lost, and there are no tears to shed. The Japanese are displaying the ferocity of the second German. In the Showa era, they are foolishly imitating Wilhelm II as the leader of the war. Previously, they were stealing secretly; now, they are looting during a fire. Their recent atrocities, such as robbing our banks and looting our people, have long placed international law and the Kellogg-Briand Pact in a position of disdain. This kind of behavior is like that of an international robber. It is like the former Germany, a threat to the world. The various atrocities that they are carrying out in the three eastern provinces of China today, who knows if they will not follow the same pattern and deal with the United Kingdom, the United States, Germany, France, and other countries in the future? Therefore, there is a public opinion in the international community that is dissatisfied with the Japanese army's atrocities. This is not necessarily because they like us or are giving us favors. It is a policy that other countries should adopt for their own self-defense. We, the people of the nation, should express our gratitude to those who uphold justice. However, if we do not fundamentally eradicate the bad habit of always relying on others to speak for us, we will definitely not be able to redeem ourselves or save ourselves. Please pay attention to this.

Alas, the sovereignty of our Republic rests with the people. It is hoped that the true will of the people will be fully expressed. We must immediately cease internal strife and jointly resist foreign insults. As an old man like myself, I long for the land of my fathers to be as stable as a rock forever. Therefore, I do not hesitate to speak out and explain the great importance of self-redemption and self-salvation to the gentlemen of our country. But what causes the most heartache is that our country today is still in a state of being brave in private quarrels but cowardly in public indignation. I hope that in the future, without the public will of the people, we will absolutely not allow a single bullet to be wasted internally. Externally, we must not hesitate to spare a single bullet. May my people be roused and may my people rise up quickly!

Important News from Tianjin

The Atrocities of the Japanese Army

Shenyang, Changchun, and Yingkou Have All Been Forcibly Occupied

Transportation Between Tianjin and Shenyang Is Now Completely Blocked

Zhang Xueliang's Remarks to Tianjin Reporters

Tianjin Dispatch: The Japanese have been plotting the Northeast problem for more than just a day or two. The Wanbaoshan Incident was actually a kind of provocation. Fortunately, our side handled it calmly, and it did not lead to an incident. Therefore, recently, they have been making a big fuss over the so-called Nakamura Incident to achieve their ambitions of aggression. It has been rumored for more than a month that the Japanese army would act freely in the Northeast, but unexpectedly, it was realized the night before. They forcibly occupied Shenyang with violence, and at the same time, they successively occupied Changchun, Yingkou, Andong, and other places. Our losses were heavy, and there were many casualties. The people of the country were all gnashing their teeth when they heard about it. Here is a brief account of the Japanese army's occupation of Shenyang, obtained from transportation circles. Recently, the Japanese army in the Northeast has been provoking us at any time and any place, which is almost unbearable. Zhang Xueliang, in order to be cautious in dealing with foreign affairs, strictly ordered the troops stationed in the area to avoid conflicts as much as possible so that the Japanese would have no excuse. The Japanese plan did not succeed, so at about 11:00 PM the night before (the 18th), twenty armed Japanese soldiers surrounded the Beining Railway station at the intersection of Sandong Bridge North Beining and the South Manchuria Railway. First, they drove away the workers inside, and then they took away all the tools for repairing the railway, using them to destroy the tracks. A total of six sections were destroyed, about several dozen feet long. At that time, the Pingji train, when traveling to this point, could not pass through and stopped east of Shenyang station. The Japanese soldiers guarded the destroyed railway, and no one was allowed to come and go. At about 12:00 AM, another part of the Japanese army shelled Beida Camp in Shenyang, causing shock throughout the city. The First Brigade, led by Wang Yizhe, stationed in Shenyang, maintained calm and adopted a policy of non-resistance and retreat. As a result, the Japanese army entered the city en masse, invaded the barracks, and set them on fire. The grain depot and the mortar factory in Beida Camp were simultaneously blown up by the Japanese army with electric current. The fire had not been extinguished by yesterday afternoon. The institutions in various provinces and cities were occupied. Zang Shiyi, the chairman of the province, and Rong Zhen, the chief of staff of the Border Defense Command, were also captured by the Japanese army. After the Japanese army entered the city, all transportation facilities, such as telegraph and telephone, were cut off. Since 4:00 AM yesterday morning, the communication facilities between Pingjin and Shenyang have been completely blocked. After the First Brigade Commander Wang Yizhe's troops entered the city, they were disarmed, and Wang also suffered misfortune. All police stations were occupied at the same time, and many police officers were killed or injured. The exact number of deaths of merchants and civilians is unknown. The whole city is in a state of chaos. It is said that the Second Division of the Japanese Army entered the city. Yesterday, reinforcements continued to arrive and advanced towards Shenyang. Changchun and Yingkou were also occupied at around 6:00 AM yesterday morning. Battalion Commander Fu, stationed in Changchun, was shot and killed by the Japanese army. In Yingkou, two Japanese trains arrived first and tied up the battalion commander, stationmaster, and police chief. Their whereabouts are still unknown. Then, they shelled the Yingkou port with artillery. Our newly built wharves were all destroyed. A Japanese naval warship was stationed there, and it is said that sailors also landed to assist the army in its operations. Yesterday, the diplomatic corps stationed in Pingjin and the reporter corps in Pingjin sent personnel to Shenyang to investigate the situation. They arrived in Huanggu Village this afternoon. As for Tianjin, after hearing the news that the Japanese army had forcibly occupied Shenyang, the party, government, and military circles convened an emergency meeting yesterday morning to discuss countermeasures. Starting today, the entire city will fly flags at half-mast for three days to mourn the compatriots who were killed. They also sent a telegram to Guangdong, asking them to put aside their prejudices and unite against foreign aggression. The attitude of the Pingjin authorities is very calm. Mayor Zhang Xueming returned to Tianjin from Peiping this morning. After meeting with Chairman Wang Shuchang, he went to Peiping in the afternoon. I met Zhang at the station, and according to him, no news can be transmitted from Shenyang City. All transportation facilities are in the hands of the Japanese army. In addition to asking the National Government for instructions, the Deputy Commander is considering ways to deal with the situation. He hopes that all sectors of society will work together and not rely solely on the government's strength. Before a solution is determined, he hopes that the citizens will continue as usual and not take any radical actions. Therefore, the situation in the city has remained normal for the past two days. Although the Beining train to Tianjin is still operating as usual this morning, it only sells tickets to Xinmin Station. It is said that many refugees from Shenyang are along the stations. There is also news that Japanese residents in Shanhaiguan are gathering in Tianjin. (September 20)

Yesterday morning, a reporter from the Tianjin Ta Kung Pao received news that Shenyang had been occupied by the Japanese army and immediately drove to Xiehe Hospital to visit Vice Commander Zhang. It was 10:00 AM. The guards and others already knew about the Shenyang Incident and were whispering to each other, appearing quite nervous. After a while, Zhang came out to meet with a recovered spirit and normal gait. His ears had also healed greatly. There were many guests waiting to see him. Zhang hurriedly told the reporter, "You have come to inquire about the news of Shenyang, right? I will tell you the truth. I have long ordered my soldiers not to resist the Japanese army's provocations. Therefore, the troops in Beida Camp were ordered to turn in their weapons and store them in the armory. At about 10:00 PM last night (the 18th), the Japanese army suddenly climbed into our camp with 300 men and opened fire. Our army was unarmed, so there was no resistance. Three people were killed. Previously, the Japanese used a locomotive to carry soldiers to the intersection of the Sino-Japanese railway in Huanggu Village and blew it up, and then retreated. Therefore, the Japanese claimed that our army destroyed the tracks of the South Manchuria Railway, which is absolutely untrue. How could we do such a thing since we are trying to avoid Japanese provocations? The consuls of various countries stationed in Shenyang can understand the truth. After the Japanese soldiers entered Beida Camp, every five to ten minutes, they fired artillery from the affiliated area, directly bombing Beida Camp and the arsenal. I immediately consulted with the Japanese Consul General Hayashi in Shenyang and asked him to stop it within five minutes. Hayashi first asked for a limit of ten minutes, and then telegraphed that it had become a military operation and that he could not stop it. Since then, the

Page 12

soldiers occupied all means of transportation, and even my residence was guarded by Japanese soldiers. However, the order was not disrupted until 6:30 AM yesterday. Our officials and civilians were not prepared to resist. I believe Chairman Zang Shiyi will do his best to maintain order in the city and prevent it from being disrupted. This matter should be handled by the government through negotiations. Japan has neither issued an ultimatum nor declared war, but has actually taken military action, which is incomprehensible. I still hope that the people will remain calm and patient and not create complications. Up to the time of the interview, the report I received was only up to 6:30 AM on the 19th." The reporter then asked about the Nakamura Incident. Zhang replied that the Japanese pointed out that the leader of the responsible group, Guan Yuhang, had been arrested in the Gendarmerie Command, and high officials such as Commander Chen Xingya had been sent to investigate. It can be seen that we must do everything according to the law. However, before the crime is clear, it is of course inconvenient to bring the suspects to justice. Moreover, negotiations on this matter are in progress, and there is absolutely no reason to resort to force.

The People of Wuhan

Organize a National Salvation Association

Vow to Resist the Atrocities of Japan

Telegraph to Guangdong to Cease Strife and Defend Against Insults

Hankou Dispatch: This time, the Japanese soldiers acted fiercely and forcibly occupied various places in Shenyang, acting violently. The people of Wuhan were very indignant and vowed to wash away the national shame. Starting on the 21st, they all wore black gauze on their arms, stopped banquets and entertainment, and various organizations flew flags at half-mast to express their grief. The Hubei Provincial Party Department Provisional Consolidation Committee, the Hankou Special City Party Department Provisional Consolidation Committee, the Pinghan Railway Special Party Department Preparatory Committee, and the Wu-Chang-Zhu-Ping Railway Special Party Department Preparatory Committee, in addition to convening emergency meetings to discuss countermeasures, also held a joint meeting at 2:00 PM on the 21st in the auditorium of the Provincial Party Department in Wuchang. Hundreds of members of the four party departments and representatives of various people's organizations in Wuhan attended the meeting. After paying their respects, the chairman, Yu Yuzhi, reported the general situation of the Japanese army's atrocities. Then, it was submitted for discussion. After discussion, it was decided to organize a national salvation association to resist the enemy together, and Wen Juntian, Zeng Juexian, and others were elected to draft the articles of association, so that they could be submitted to the second general meeting on the 22nd for approval and establishment. It is said that the association will set up action and propaganda committees to facilitate the process. The candidates for the committee will also be elected on the 22nd and will start working immediately. If necessary, branch associations can also be set up in Yichang, Wuxue, and other cities, so that we can work together to save the crisis. In addition, the Provincial Party Department sent a telegram to the Central National Government on the 21st, requesting that a strategy be quickly decided, and also sent a telegram to the Guangdong authorities, urging them to immediately cease internal strife and jointly face the national crisis. The Hankou Municipal Party Department and the Pinghan Railway Special Party Department also expressed the same views (the telegram is omitted due to space constraints).

Anti-Japanese Excitement in Xuzhou

An Anti-Japanese Meeting of More Than 20,000 People

The Entire City Flies Flags at Half-Mast to Express Grief

Xuzhou Dispatch: The Japanese army trampled on the eastern provinces, and Xuzhou received a radio message on the evening of the 19th. The local newspapers of the 20th were filled with reports, and the public was suddenly tense. The Party Department was preparing to commemorate Zhu Zhixin's martyrdom and promote the national goods movement, so it issued an emergency notice to hold an anti-Japanese rally at the same time. Today (the 21st) morning, people from all walks of life gathered at the large sports field of the People's Education Center. Most of the organizations, groups, and schools participated fully, with about 20,000 people attending. The meeting began at 9:00 AM. The chairman of the Party Committee, Xu Ximing, reported the significance of the meeting. Then, representatives of various groups gave speeches, which were passionate and tearful. After discussing the proposals, four important telegrams were unanimously passed: (1) Telegraph to the Central Government, urging the implementation of revolutionary diplomacy against Japan; (2) Telegraph to Guangdong, urging them to cease military operations immediately and unite against foreign aggression; (3) Send a telegram to the whole country, urging everyone to form powerful armed organizations; (4) Telegraph to the Central Government, urging the dismissal and investigation of Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting, and warning the Northeast Border Defense Commander. The telegrams were sent on the spot. The meeting ended at 11:00 AM and a parade was held. The entire group set off, with a total of 132 groups, plus citizens, the line stretched for seven or eight miles, encircling the city's railway station, shouting slogans like thunder. It dispersed at 3:00 PM in the afternoon. Today, the entire city flies flags at half-mast to express grief, and various anti-Japanese slogans are posted in front of all shops. (September 21)

Zhejiang Provincial Party and Government Authorities

Request Preparation of Strength to Confront Japan

The Zhejiang Provincial Party and Government authorities, in response to the Japanese army's forcible occupation of various places in our eastern provinces, held an emergency talk today (September 22) and decided: (1) To telegraph the Central Government to seriously negotiate with Japan and prepare to deal with it with strength; (2) To telegraph condolences to Vice Commander Zhang and all the military and civilians in the Northeast; (3) To telegraph to the Guangdong comrades, urging them to consider the national crisis, eliminate personal prejudices, and unite against Japan. The telegram to the Central Government is recorded below: To the Nanjing Central Executive Committee, the National Government, and the Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force: Having read the telegrams from Your Committee and Vice Commander Zhang, and having read the reports in various newspapers, we are shocked to learn that Japan attacked and destroyed our Beida Camp, occupied our Shenyang, killed our military officers, plundered our people, and recently occupied Changchun, Liaoyang, Andong, Yingkou, and Lianshan Bay on September 18th and 19th, and has even shown signs of moving into Shanhaiguan. All parties, including the Party, government, military, and civilians, are filled with anger. It is believed that Japan has been plotting to seize Manchuria and Mongolia for more than a day. Unexpectedly, they have launched an unprovoked invasion, looting freely, disregarding world justice, and destroying East Asian peace. They dare to set a bad international precedent and disregard the Kellogg-Briand Pact. Their intention is nothing more than to take advantage of our natural disasters, the prevalence of internal strife, and the belief that we are unable to resist and can do whatever they want. Therefore, compared to the previous invasion of Jinan, it is even more barbaric. Such humiliation and pain is irreconcilable. We ask that the diplomatic authorities be ordered to seriously negotiate with Japan, and the military authorities across the country be ordered to prepare their strength and not make any further concessions, lest we suffer the disaster of national subjugation and racial extinction. This urgent telegram expresses our utmost anticipation. Signed, Zhejiang Provincial Party Department and Provincial Government (seal).

Local Dispatch

Songjiang

Fellow Songjiang Natives in Beijing Establish the Yunjian Guide Newspaper: The fellow Songjiang natives in Beijing have recently been concerned that the various undertakings of their hometown have been progressing slowly. Therefore, they plan to raise funds to establish a small-scale publication dedicated to commenting on Songjiang matters, so as to promote construction plans. The initiators, Pu Mengjiu, Gao Liangzuo, Lu Shunong, Lu Buqing, Xu Weisheng, Gu Wenbin, Gu Liquan, Chen Shuzhen, and others, have decided to publish the "Yunjian Guide" twice a month, which will be printed in Nanjing. The office will be temporarily located at No. 2 Chenghouli, across from the Central Party Department. The expenses are currently borne by the initiators. When the number of members increases in the future, the expenses will be maintained by the association fees. The staff has been determined, and preparations are underway. It is scheduled to be published on October 1st, and it has been submitted to the Party and government authorities for record. It is said that the newspaper is completely open for discussion and welcomes Songjiang people to submit letters to discuss Songjiang matters.

Suzhou

A Grocery Store in Xiangshan Township Was Robbed: On the night of the 21st, three bandit ships arrived in Chuli Township, Xiangshan. More than 20 bandits, each carrying firearms, swarmed into Zhou Dinglong's grocery store to rob it. They also injured the shop owner, Zhou Shangqing, his mother, Wang, and his wife, Zhong. More than 600 yuan in silver dollars were robbed.

Various Circles in Suzhou Are Aroused Against Japan: The county government will convene an emergency meeting yesterday (22nd) regarding the Japanese army's invasion of the eastern provinces, deciding on: (1) Setting the 26th as a propaganda day, with all schools above middle school suspending classes and promoting propaganda as much as possible; (2) Convening a mass meeting on the 25th; (3) Drafting and issuing telegrams; (4) Requiring all officials and civilians to wear black gauze on their arms today (23rd) to express their grief, with the entire county flying flags at half-mast for three days.

Wuxi

Rumors are rife about opening the Eastern Dam, and the collapse of the Eastern Dam in Liyang. Previously, there were widespread rumors about opening up the Su (Suzhou) and Chang (Changzhou) areas, causing great panic among the people. They have been sending telegrams to the provincial government requesting a halt to protect the lives of tens of millions of people. The Director of Civil Affairs also recognizes the importance of the dam and has dispatched a provincial security team to protect it. However, on the 19th of this month, a boat traveling from Liyang to Gaochun saw slogans calling for the demolition of the Eastern Dam plastered on the walls of Gaochun. Subsequently, a Mr. Wang from Liyang copied the slogans and returned to Liyang to report it. The Director of the Construction Bureau, Shi Ziquan, upon receiving the report, urgently consulted with County Magistrate Chen Xi, who immediately dispatched a company of the provincial security team to protect it. Many local residents are also guarding the dam day and night. Yesterday, Chen Rongquan, the manager of the Yonggu Shipping Bureau in Wuxi, received an urgent telegram from Liyang stating that tens of thousands of Anhui residents had gathered at the Eastern Dam, forcefully attempting to open it, and that the situation was urgent. When County Magistrate Chen of Wuxi heard about this, he also telegraphed Liyang to inquire and confirmed that it was indeed happening, although not as widespread as rumored. Qian Sunqing, the chairman of the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce, at 9 PM that evening, in conjunction with the Flood Relief Committee, urgently telegraphed the provincial government, stating that it concerned the lives and property of tens of millions of people in Jiangnan and urgently requested the immediate dispatch of troops to protect it. They also sent telegrams to the counties of Wuxi, Liyang, and Gaochun, instructing them to pay attention to defense and not be negligent in the slightest. Chairman Qian also sent a quick letter to the Liyang Chamber of Commerce, scheduling a joint meeting of the relevant county chambers of commerce at the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce on October 1st to discuss relief measures. The county authorities also decided that night to hire several steamships, keep the fires burning, and be ready to depart. If an alert is received from Liyang, Wuxi will consider dispatching police and large units of investigators, and negotiate with the local troops to rush to assist in protecting the dam to safeguard the lives and property of tens of millions of people.

Anti-Japanese National Salvation Mass Meeting Wuxi's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Mass Meeting was held yesterday afternoon at 1 PM in the open space below the train station. More than 100,000 people from all walks of life attended. Chairman Li Tiping passed the following resolutions: (1) Send a telegram to the whole country to unanimously call for a cessation of hostilities and peace to jointly resist foreign aggression. (2) Send a telegram to the central government urging the implementation of revolutionary diplomacy and the dismissal of Wang Zhengting, who is humiliating the country and forfeiting its rights. (3) Send a telegram to the central government instructing the entire country to prepare for war against Japan. (4) Send a telegram to the central government to issue a clear order to the entire country to implement a permanent economic severance with Japan.

Jiangyin

Yi, Education Committee Investigator, Investigates the Nanching Expulsion-of-Principal Incident. The Education Department dispatched Provincial Inspector Yi Jianlou to Cheng (Jiangyin) to investigate the Nanching Middle School's expulsion of principal incident triggered by students. Inspector Yi first arrived in Shanghai on the 16th to investigate the Nanching school property. On the 18th, he came to Cheng. For several days, teachers and students have been presenting the situation to Inspector Yi. On the 20th, he met with County Magistrate Peng at the county government. In the afternoon, he held a meeting of teachers and staff at Nanching. Inspector Yi indicated that an agreement had been reached with Feng Taiyuan regarding finances, and payments would be made according to the agreement. If the student self-governing body obstructs, he would be responsible. He said that after he returns to the province to report, if financial problems arise, County Magistrate Peng would be responsible. However, Feng Taiyuan only has a remaining balance of over seven thousand yuan, which can only support operations for two months. As for future finances, a telegram has been sent to Chen Gucen, the school board director in charge of finances, to return to Cheng to handle the matter. In the afternoon, the student self-governing body requested a meeting to ask Inspector Yi to explain, but Inspector Yi refused. Inspector Yi will need to investigate the expulsion-of-principal incident for several more days before returning to the province to report.

Changzhou

County Party Headquarters Emergency Meeting The Wu County Party Headquarters convened an emergency meeting at 9 PM on the 21st, chaired by Gao Bozhen. The items discussed were: (1) How to respond to the national crisis of the violent Japanese occupation of Shenyang and other places. The following resolutions were passed: (A) Submit a petition to the central government, ordering a general mobilization of the national army, navy, and air force to formally declare war on Japan as a final response. (B) Send a telegram to comrades in Guangdong to cease hostilities and make peace, uniting against foreign aggression. (C) Convene a county-wide Anti-Japanese National Salvation Mass Meeting to unanimously oppose Japan and serve as a backing for the government. (D) Order all lower-level party headquarters and people's organizations to expand anti-Japanese propaganda and intensify anti-Japanese work. (E) Send a telegram to the whole country to advocate unity. (2) Should the date for the county-wide Anti-Japanese National Salvation Mass Meeting be confirmed? It was decided that it would be held at 9 AM on the 24th of this month at the public sports field, and a preparatory meeting would be convened on the morning of the day before.

Nantong

Fierce Battle Between Police and Bandits in Dayu Town More than 20 bandit ships, carrying over 300 bandits, suddenly arrived in Dayu Town, Juegang, at 2 AM on the 21st. They landed, hoping to loot grain and supplies from the residents. They were intercepted by the police and local militia, and fierce fighting continued until dawn, at which point the bandits fled by ship. The losses were minor.

Collecting Evidence of Japanese Ship Causing Disaster The Yijin Maru of the Dalian Steamship Company struck and sank a Xu Hui cargo ship on the Nantong section of the Yangtze River. The county government reported this to the provincial government, which then consulted with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to negotiate with the Japanese ambassador. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs then approved the Japanese ambassador's reply, which stated that the Dalian Steamship Company claimed that the sailing ship did not have its sails up at the time. When the Yijin Maru discovered the sailing ship in its path, it had already approached the ship's vicinity. The ship immediately reversed and dropped anchor, but it was unable to avoid the collision. Therefore, the Dalian Steamship Company should not bear any responsibility for this collision. The captain of the Yijin Maru signed a written statement acknowledging that the case would be resolved in Shanghai when he left port in Tianshenggang, but he claimed that he was coerced by the local maritime officials. On the 21st, County Magistrate Zhang received an order to investigate each item in this case and collect sufficient evidentiary documents to submit to the ministry for rebuttal.

Pinghu

Strange Death of a Soil Vendor Qian A'si, a well-known soil vendor from Pinghu's East City River Beach (also known as Xiang A'si), was reported to the county government on the 19th for allegedly selling opium. The county government arrested Qian and found a package of red pills. The next day, during interrogation, he was sentenced to four months in prison and fined one hundred yuan, to be executed in prison. Unexpectedly, upon being sent to the prison, he cried out and died. The truth of his death is subject to various rumors. Some say he committed suicide out of fear of punishment, while others say that his concubine, Qian Yang'shi, laced his food with poison. The truth will never be know. However, after Qian died, he bled from seven orifices, suggesting that Yang'shi was likely involved in killing him. At 3 PM on the 21st, the county government sent Examiner Song, along with a forensic official, to conduct an examination. The examination concluded that he died from poisoning. Yang'shi was arrested and will be interrogated further.

丨Record of the Awards Ceremony丨

The awards and closing ceremony of the city's Second Municipal Games was held at 4 PM yesterday at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. Mayor Zhang, Director Xu of the Education Bureau, Director Hu of the Health Bureau, Secretary Feng of the Public Security Bureau, guests, and over 500 athletes and winners attended. The ceremony was performed as usual. Mayor Zhang delivered a training speech, roughly stating that the results of this Municipal Games had four advantages: 1. The number of participants was greater than the first Games, indicating that physical education in Shanghai has become more popular than before. 2. The female athletes who participated in this competition achieved special results, proving that they have worked hard in the past year. 3. This Games broke national records, indicating that technology has improved since advancements. 4. This Games included swimming and national health events, which further highlights Shanghai's special achievements. I hope that there will be progress every year in the future. Currently, our country is suffering from natural disasters and man-made disasters, and internal troubles are urgent. In addition, with foreign aggression, considering the future, one cannot help but feel a chill. I sincerely hope that society and the government will work together to restore the entire national spirit, endure hardship, and accumulate strength in order to deal with everything. This Games was hosted by the Education Bureau and received much assistance from all walks of life, which is deeply appreciated. The health exercises of the municipal government staff had over 200 participants with good results. Therefore, we can see that the student emphasized sports. The government encourages the same, and all sectors further their efforts. Future achievements will have new records, and it will not be difficult for Shanghai to become a model city that focuses on sports. Next, Secretary Feng of the Public Security Bureau spoke, roughly stating that only with strong physiques and full spirits can people undertake great things. He hoped that people would pay attention to sports and work hard to exercise. Finally, Director Xu reported two thoughts on this Games: (1) Judging from the records of various sports, the progress of athletes in general is rapid, especially the progress of female athletes, which is even faster and worth commemorating. (2) Under the current serious state, I hope everyone will work as hard on all construction projects as they do on sports. Not only can they resist foreign aggression, but in other words, there is nothing that cannot be achieved one day. Next, Director Xu gave out the awards, and the ceremony was adjourned.

Local News

Shanghai Educational Circles Face the National Crisis

Implement Military Training, Economically Sever Ties with Japan, Spiritually Unite as One

Jiaotong University Anti-Japanese Movement

Xujiahui Jiaotong University held a general meeting of all students at 10 AM yesterday, resolving to suspend classes in order to promote awareness to all sectors. An Anti-Japanese Committee was specially formed, divided into four departments: general affairs, discipline, propaganda, and lectures, as well as attending representatives. The lecture department divided the students within the school into numbered teams, totaling 70 teams, each with 10 people. At 2 PM on the 22nd, they went to Xujiahui, Fahua Town, Longhua, and the Southern City, where the audience was extremely enthusiastic. The propaganda department printed various slogans, leaflets, and multiple circular telegrams. The department also has an information section that specializes in investigating news of the Japanese army from various newspapers in order to promote awareness early in the morning. They also went to various schools to discuss procedures. However, fearing that students might slack off during the suspension of classes, special discipline department personnel were dispatched to supervise and monitor. A sign-in sheet was placed at the school gate, and students entering and leaving the school were required to sign in to prevent evasion. Representatives Yuan Bingnan, Cheng Weinan, Liu Liangzhan, and three others were sent to the municipal government yesterday to meet with Mayor Zhang for talks.

Students of Jinan University Overflowing with Passionate Indignation

Students of Jinan University, angered by the Japanese military's unreasonable and forceful occupation of the Eastern Provinces, convened an emergency meeting last night. In addition to uniting with various universities in Shanghai for joint action, they also sent telegrams to overseas Chinese compatriots in various regions, expressing a serious anti-Japanese stance. Meanwhile, the university's student army, invigorated and disciplined, is on standby. Furthermore, President Zheng Hongnian, in an earnest address at the university's weekly memorial service the day before yesterday, emphasized that this incident is truly a matter of China's survival and called for a comprehensive strategy to address it, offering it to the government for reference and urging the people to seek international adjudication. The strategy advocated by President Zheng is currently being drafted, encompassing the following aspects: (1) the accumulated causes of recent events since the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-95, (2) the opportunities China missed at the Paris Peace Conference, (3) the process of transforming the Three Eastern Provinces into provinces, (4) a history of transportation in the Three Eastern Provinces, (5) sketches of key Japanese figures, (6) international attitudes, and (7) strategies for response.

Wuben Girls' Middle School National Salvation Assembly

Wuben Girls' Middle School held a national salvation assembly yesterday (the 22nd) at one o'clock in the afternoon, gathering all teachers and students in the gymnasium. Principal Wang Xiaoying first reported on the purpose of the assembly, followed by speeches from teachers such as Cao Yihua. The following resolutions were passed: (1) cease all entertainment and amusements, (2) implement economic severance, (3) implement military training, and (4) wear badges of unity.

Students from Major Middle Schools and Universities Hold Joint Meeting

Shanghai Hujiang University convened a joint meeting of students from various universities in Shanghai at the YMCA on Sichuan Road at two o'clock yesterday afternoon. Representatives from over twenty schools, including Hujiang, Jinan, Fudan, Law School, Guanghua, Daxia, Zhonggong, Labor University, Chizhi, Tongwen College, Soochow Law School, Tongji, Law and Politics College, and Shanghai Art College, attended. The representatives discussed and drafted resolutions, deciding to hold an anti-Japanese national salvation representative assembly of Shanghai students at Soochow Law School at two o'clock this afternoon.

Moreover, various middle schools in Shanghai initiated a joint conference of Shanghai middle schools to discuss all defensive measures and plan to join the anti-Japanese national salvation efforts of various university students to strengthen their forces. The joint conference of Shanghai middle schools is scheduled to be held at the Hujiang Affiliated Middle School this afternoon.

Local News

The Entire City Will Fly Flags at Half-Mast Today in Mourning

Citizens' Assembly to be Held on the 26th

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce issued a notice to all commercial organizations, companies, and businesses in the city, stating that the Japanese military's forceful occupation of key areas in Liaoning and Jilin, resulting in the massacre of numerous military personnel and civilians, is a deeply painful and unforgettable event. The Standing Committee has resolved to fly flags at half-mast and suspend banquets and entertainment for one day on the afternoon of the 23rd to express mourning. All merchants and residents of the city should uniformly comply with this measure. This notice is hereby published for your information.

The Shanghai Special District Citizens' Federation issued an emergency notice yesterday, stating that due to the Japanese military's invasion and occupation of the Northeast, and the brutal killing of compatriots, an order has been received from the central government to fly flags at half-mast on the 23rd of this month. All stores, firms, factories, and residents throughout the city should uniformly express their mourning and must comply with this notice.

Yesterday's Delegates' Assembly of Various Groups

Request the National Government to Issue a General Mobilization Order

Expand the Anti-Japanese Association...Organize Volunteer Army

Those Who Disrupt the Boycott Movement Will Be Executed Without Mercy

Citizens' Assembly Scheduled for the 26th

The Shanghai All-Circles Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese Committee convened a delegates' assembly of various circles at 9:00 AM yesterday in the City Chamber of Commerce hall at Tianhou Temple Bridge. Over 5,000 attendees included representatives from various circles such as Hu Shuhua, Wang Xiaolai, and Wang Yansong, as well as over 800 organizations from various industries and student groups, including Jiaotong University, Soochow University, and the Law School. The atmosphere at the assembly was extremely passionate. The details of the meeting are recorded as follows:

Assembly Staff: Presidium: Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Hou Dachun, Tao Baichuan, Lu Jingshi; Recorders: Feng Yixian, Xue Guangqian; Master of Ceremonies: Yuan Hongjun.

Assembly Order: (1) All stand at attention; (2) Sing the party anthem; (3) Pay the highest respects to the Party and National Flag and the portrait of the Premier with three bows; (4) The Chairman reverently reads the Premier's will (Wang Yansong); (5) Observe three minutes of silence to mourn the deceased officials and civilians; (6) Chairman's report, Tao Baichuan; (7) Discussion of proposals; (8) Ad hoc motions; (9) Speeches from various sectors; (10) Shout slogans; (11) Adjournment.

Chairman's Report: Chairman Tao Baichuan reported: "Distinguished representatives, today the Shanghai All-Circles Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese Committee has convened a delegates' assembly of various groups in Shanghai. Its most important significance lies in this time of grief, indignation, life-or-death crisis, to examine whether the blood of the citizens of Shanghai has turned cold, whether the organization of the various groups in Shanghai is sound, and whether the citizens of Shanghai are still asleep, not thinking of rising up to resist Japan. Seeing the enthusiastic attendance at the meeting, it shows the passionate indignation of the citizens of Shanghai and the soundness of the organization. If all the people of the country can be as grief-stricken as the citizens of Shanghai, and if we use the heads and hot blood of our 400 million compatriots to fight the 60 million Japanese, what do we have to fear? This time, the Japanese atrocities have brazenly disregarded the great disapproval of the world, deploying heavy troops to occupy the Eastern Provinces, disrupting peace in East Asia. Their pretext is the Nakamura Incident. Whether Nakamura exists as a person and whether Nakamura traveled to the Eastern Provinces, there is still no conclusive evidence presented. However, the Japanese did not use formal channels to resolve the issue, and instead deployed troops to occupy Shenyang, Changchun, Yingkou, Jilin, and other places. The reason they did not declare war is that they want to imitate the old trick of the Soviet Union two years ago, using artillery to bombard the Northeast, first occupying the territory, and then negotiating with us. Under the city's alliance, the Japanese are bound to win. From this, we can know that the Japanese dispatch of troops to the Eastern Provinces this time, the Nakamura Incident, is only a propaganda material. The true intention is to annex the Northeast and conquer China. Therefore, only the power of the entire Chinese nation, rising up to resist Japan, is sufficient to save China and protect the nation. Even if we do not consider the current life and death, we should also think about future generations, raising our arms and sacrificing ourselves to serve the country. Some people say that with China's current weakness, there is really no way to resist the Japanese atrocities. The only way is to request a third country to mediate. However, mediation must first have self-defense actions. In the face of Japan's barbaric challenge, our army does not engage in legitimate defense and adheres to the principle of absolute non-resistance. The Japanese advance one step, and we retreat two steps. In this state, what self-defense is there, and what opportunity is there for mediation? Even if we put this aside, is there fair judgment in the third-party mediation? According to the words of U.S. Secretary of State Stimson, the actions of the Japanese this time have not violated the Kellogg-Briand Pact, so the signatory countries cannot speak out on this basis. Japan's dispatch of troops to occupy the Eastern Provinces, all actions, everyone knows, is no different from a state of war. The United States, as the initiator of the Peace Pact, still makes this fallacy. Other countries are even more out of the question. Does the world still have reason and justice? Therefore, our desire for third-party mediation, our desire to fight for the existence of reason and justice, is tantamount to surrendering to Japan. We must first have the sacrifice of some people, fight the Japanese, otherwise, without any resistance, we are willing to surrender. In terms of China's current position, the Japanese will also reject and refuse to accept it. Whether we advocate war, whether we advocate peace, or whether we beg for surrender, we must prepare the whole country consistently. I hope that compatriots will prepare themselves." Representative Report: Zheng Chengqing, a representative for appealing to the capital, reported, in brief, that he was recommended by the Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese Committee, together with Wang Hanliang, Li Yongxiang, Tang Junsheng, Chen Yasheng, and other four comrades, to appeal to the central government in the capital. They were received by Wu Zhihui, Zhang Jingjiang, Dai Jitao, and other members of the Central Committee. The purpose of the representatives' petition was threefold: (1) Concentrate national military forces and unite against foreign aggression; (2) Request the Central Government to implement revolutionary diplomacy; (3) Implement national economic severance. Comrade Dai Jitao gave a sincere and satisfactory reply, stating that according to information from the central government, the Guangdong government will soon make a peaceful statement. In addition, the Central Government showed the representatives that there are three things it hopes all compatriots across the country will consistently follow: (1) Except for the Communist Party, which endangers the nation, all compatriots across the country should not be divided and should unite; (2) In addition to the anti-Japanese movement, the people of the country must work harder to relieve disaster to save compatriots; (3) Comrades of this party, at this time when the survival of the country is at stake, should eliminate their opinions and jointly face national difficulties.

Discussion of Various Items: (1) The association should issue a declaration, resolved to have Hu Shuhua, Tao Baichuan, Yan E'sheng, Zhao Shusheng, and Wang Pingnan draft it; (2) Telegraphed to the National Government to immediately issue a general mobilization order for the army, navy, and air force to expel Japanese troops from the country and restore lost territory, resolved, passed; (3) A circular telegram was sent to the country to unite forces and unanimously resist Japan, resolved, passed; (4) To organize a national salvation volunteer corps to recruit members to resist foreign aggression together, resolved, passed, to be handled by the Executive Committee; (5) The Anti-Japanese Aid-the-Overseas-Chinese Committee should change its name to the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Committee due to factual needs, and expand the organization to stipulate that there be sixty-one members. The original thirty-seven members will be supplemented by twenty-four members. The following twenty-four people were elected as committee members: Shi Liangcai, Wu Mai, Wang Boqi, Wu Zhihao, Zhao Jijin, Xu Wei, Zhu Xuefan, Lu Muqin, Wang Changyuan, Gu Ruofeng, Gong Yuting, Fu Dewei, Yu Zhongxian, Luo Qinghua, Ma Shaoquan, Zhang Zilian, Liu Qinqian, Ren Jinping, Liu Zhan'en, Lin Kanghou, Chu Huiseng, Xie Fusheng, Dong Xianfu, Hu Shuhua. Chen Haiqiu, Xu Jiqing, Ye Jiaxing, Zhao Shusheng, Yu Zhenhui, Wang Yuxiang, Long Peiyun, Wang Pingnan, Qiu Zitong, Xu Mujue, Cao Zhigong, Jin Chuxiang, Zhang Tianbai, Zheng Hairuo, Guanghua, Daxia University, and representatives of students from Tongwen College and seventeen other people, as alternate members. If a member is absent from a meeting three times, he will be removed from his post, and the alternate member will be replaced in order; (6) Discussing the holding of a citizens' assembly on a regular basis, and on that day the city will suspend business for one day to express condolences, resolved, passed, scheduled to be held on September 26; (7) A telegram was sent to the National Government to return the Japanese disaster relief goods and money, and the people themselves will raise donations for relief, resolved, passed; (8) Thoroughly implement economic severance with Japan, resolved, passed, those who undermine it will be executed without mercy; (9) The remaining cases that have not been discussed shall be handled by the Executive Committee, resolved, passed.

The above-mentioned cases are indeed urgent measures to defend against insults and save ourselves. We humbly believe that people who save the country share the same heart, and there is no turning back. We earnestly hope that compatriots across the country will rise up together, on the one hand, urge the government to concentrate its forces, consolidate the army, and preserve the territory, and fight the violent Japan to the final victory, on the other hand, strictly organize, actively promote thorough cargo clearance, and earnestly resist Japan, to promote the self-awareness of the people of that country and awaken the sympathy of the human race in the world. The matter of survival is related to life and death. We express our declaration and hope that it will be made public.

Today, Entertainment Venues Will Suspend Business to Express Condolences

The Municipal Bureau of Education Called a Meeting with the Entertainment Industry Yesterday to Discuss

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education convened an emergency meeting at the bureau at 3:00 p.m. yesterday, gathering over thirty people from various circles, including stage theaters, storytellers, entertainers, and tabloid newspapers, to discuss concrete measures for national salvation propaganda.

The meeting was chaired by Li Dachao, section chief of the Bureau of Education. After the meeting was held as usual, the chairman first reported on the purpose of the meeting, and then made a simple speech to the effect that Japan relies on its strength to insult our country, invade our territory, and seize our land, which did not start today. However, the authorities of our country have repeatedly made concessions to maintain peace, but the Japanese government's ambitions are rampant, and it has brutally occupied Shenyang, intending to annex the Northeast, lost all humanity, and destroyed reason. If the government and people of our country do not unite to rise up, jointly plan to resist Japan, and make serious representations, then not only will they not be able to contain the realization of their ambitions on the continent, but when will the current humiliation be redressed? This is truly a critical juncture for the survival of our nation. All of you present are part of the Republic of China. You should have a considerable understanding of the incident of the Japanese army's occupation of our country, and you should unite to propagate everywhere, awaken the people, and deeply awaken national salvation. The above remarks aroused the sympathy and indignation of the participants. Soon, discussions began.

Four Resolutions: Four resolutions were made: (1) On the 23rd, all entertainment agencies will suspend entertainment for one day to express condolences; (2) All drama troupes, theaters, entertainment storytelling groups, and tabloid newspapers will all compile, perform, narrate, and publish reports on the atrocities of the Japanese soldiers, and conduct anti-Japanese propaganda; (3) All sectors will jointly organize an anti-Japanese propaganda national salvation association; (4) If problems arise in the second and third items, the municipal government should be responsible for handling them. The meeting was adjourned.

At present, we should wait patiently for the government's prudent measures. If necessary, we will give up our lives and drive out, which we will not hesitate to do. We also hope that the government authorities will, within the scope of possibility, clearly announce all the details of diplomacy, so that the people of the country can clearly understand the truth and be more determined to live and die together. The Shanghai Education Circles National Salvation Federation respectfully appeals (the telegram to the League of Nations and the peoples of various countries should not be published for the time being)

Mayor Zhang

Hope That Citizens Will Remain Calm

A reporter from Huadong News Agency interviewed Mayor Zhang of the Municipal Government yesterday, because Japanese in Shanghai are quite provocative towards the Chinese side, hoping to cause unfortunate incidents and use them as an excuse to send troops to Shanghai. Secretary Guo was sent by Zhang to receive the reporter. According to Secretary Guo, the Japanese provocation is obviously ulterior, but our people must remain calm and not act rashly, lest they be taken advantage of by the other side. After the incident of Japanese atrocities was launched, the municipal government secretly ordered the Public Security Bureau to strictly prevent the occurrence of unfortunate incidents. Now, the National Government has also issued a telegram to all subordinates to this effect, protecting the safety of the Japanese on the one hand and persuading the people to wait for the government's proper negotiations on the other hand.

However, it will still maintain a calm attitude towards the Japanese military's demonstrations and provocations in order to avoid lightly initiating disputes.

Methods of the Five-Person Anti-Japanese Group

The Five-Person Anti-Japanese Group's public notice states: Respected Sirs, Japan has been scheming for years to destroy China. Over the past decade, its intentions have become increasingly clear. Recently, it has even dispatched troops without cause, occupying Shenyang and other important locations in the eastern provinces, implementing a policy of annexation. National subjugation is imminent. We who are determined to save the nation lack the strength to wield weapons. We intend to do what we can to fulfill our duty as citizens. Considering that Japanese goods rely on China as their sole outlet, if we can cut off that outlet, Japan will inevitably collapse. Therefore, we invite comrades to passively resist and boycott. The method is to first gather five comrades, swear an oath to heaven, and henceforth, regarding clothing, food, shelter, and transportation, except for cultural and medical items, and other things that Japanese goods are the only alternative, no longer purchase them at all, until the day when Japan abolishes all unequal treaties with China and ceases all acts of aggression and occupation against China. All members who join this five-person group must each invite four other comrades with patriotic spirit to form a group. These four people must also each invite four other comrades to form a group. By inviting and expanding in this manner, we aim for the five-person anti-Japanese group to spread throughout the country, using its patriotic sincerity to implement economic severance. However, this organization only guarantees its oath with personal integrity. There is no such thing as a general group or branch group, nor are there any meetings or gatherings. There are no penalty clauses for members who violate the oath. As for raising funds, opening factories, revitalizing industry, etc., members are free to handle these matters on their own, which are not within the scope of this group's organizational purpose, so there are no membership fees or donations, etc. If each group member can act with enthusiasm and determination, advancing separately and persevering to the end, the expected results can be considerable within a year. Within five years, Japan will inevitably suffer a major blow, and it will be easy and effortless for us. Anyone can implement this, and success depends on human effort. We hope that patriotic people will enthusiastically promote and cooperate in persevering. As long as there is breath, this aspiration will not cease. This is most sincere. This notice is issued by the Five-Person Anti-Japanese Group. Municipal Joint Conference Resolution

New Voice Society Reprint

Tanaka's Active Policy of Aggression Towards Manchuria and Mongolia

Attachment Printing must be contacted before the end of the month

Japan's seizure of the three eastern provinces by force this time is based on the active policy of aggression towards Manchuria and Mongolia by the Tanaka Cabinet of that country. The so-called Meiji Emperor's legacy strategy is to conquer Taiwan in the first stage, conquer Korea in the second stage, and destroy Manchuria and Mongolia in the third stage, so as to conquer all of China and make the southern seas and the entire Asian belt of different clothes fear us (Japan claims) and look up to us. This is its clear proof. This policy is divided into (1) the active policy towards Manchuria and Mongolia, (2) the territory of Manchuria and Mongolia and China, (3) the active policy towards Inner and Outer Mongolia, (4) the Korean immigration reward and protection policy, (5) the new continent development and the Manchuria and Mongolia Railway, (6) the Tongliao-Jehol railway, (7) the Taonan-Solun railway, (8) a part of the Changtao railway, (9) the Jihui Railway, (10) the national policy centered on the Jihui Line and the Sea of Japan, (11) the nature of the Jihui Road project and its incidental rights and interests, (12) the Hunchun-Hailing railway, (13) the Manchuria and Mongolia trade doctrine, (14) the construction of large shipping companies centered on Dalian, (15) the implementation of the gold standard, (16) the welcome of third-country investment in Manchuria and Mongolia, (17) the South Manchuria Railway Company must change its management, (18) the steel problem, (19) the oil problem, (20) the ammonium sulfate agricultural fertilizer and other problems, (21) the soda and soda ash business, (22) tungsten and aluminum business, (23) the necessity of establishing the Takushoku Province, (24) the Great Liu River basin, (25) the defense against Chinese immigration intrusion, (26) the independent management of hospitals and schools, etc., a total of two volumes and six chapters. All invasion policies concerning politics, military affairs, economy, culture, and transportation were previously obtained by the New Voice News Agency on the fourth floor of Daxin Fang, next to the Sanma Road Shilou Daxin Silk and Satin Bureau, and reprinted 30,000 copies, which were distributed to all walks of life. Now the agency, with Japan's implementation of the seizure of Manchuria and Mongolia, is reprinting this policy on a large scale to raise awareness. All agencies, schools, groups, and businesses, if they wish to reprint the attachment, will only be charged a paper fee of four yuan per hundred copies. They must contact the New Voice News Agency before the 30th of this month in order to compile and print them, so that they know that Japan's atrocities are a predetermined plan, not a temporary conflict.

Civilian Boatmen's Union

Reorganization About to Begin

Methods Already Passed

The Executive Committee of this city resolved at yesterday's standing meeting to pass two types of regulations: the Measures for the Reorganization of the Civilian Boatmen's Union and the Organizational Rules for the Reorganization Committee of the Shanghai Citizen Civilian Boatmen's Union. Excerpts are as follows:

Draft Measures for the Reorganization of the Civilian Boatmen's Union (1) Dispatch personnel to the Public Utilities Bureau to investigate the general situation of civilian boats in this city and the number already registered. (2) Summon the heads of various labor unions that already exist and are suitable for the organizational rules of civilian boatmen to come to the meeting for discussions. (3) Select reorganization personnel and suspend the activities of their original labor unions. (4) Appoint reorganization committee members and instructors to establish a reorganization committee. (5) Set a reorganization time limit (limited to three months). (6) Those who have the qualifications to be members of the Civilian Boatmen's Union but do not yet have an organization must register with the reorganization committee within the time limit and await organization. (7) Other matters shall be determined during the preparation stage of the reorganization.

Draft Organizational Rules for the Reorganization Committee of the Shanghai Citizen Civilian Boatmen's Union Article 1. The Reorganization Committee of the Shanghai Citizen Civilian Boatmen's Union (hereinafter referred to as the Reorganization Committee) is under the guidance of the Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang and the supervision of the Bureau of Social Affairs, reorganizing the existing labor unions of civilian boatmen in this city to establish the Shanghai Citizen Civilian Boatmen's Union. Article 2. The Reorganization Committee shall have one instructor and seven reorganization committee members, who shall be appointed by the Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang. Article 3. The organization of the Reorganization Committee is as follows: A. Three standing committee members, B. One director of the general affairs section, C. One director of the registration section, D. One director of the investigation section, E. One director of the guidance section. The above-mentioned staff members shall be elected by the members of the Reorganization Committee. Article 4. The functions and powers of the Reorganization Committee are as follows: A. Reorganization matters of the original labor unions, B. Organizational matters of the labor union, C. Registration matters of new and old members, D. Other related reorganization matters. Article 5. The duties of the standing committee members are as follows: A. Convene meetings and serve as chairman, B. Foreign affairs and contact, C. Review documents and examine draft documents, D. Manage the income and expenditure of the economy. Article 6. The duties of the general affairs section are as follows: A. Drafting and proofreading various documents, B. Keeping various documents and forms of the association, C. Managing the general affairs of the association, D. Matters not belonging to other sections. Article 7. The duties of the registration section are as follows: A. Registration matters of labor union members, B. Compiling statistical reports, C. Other registration matters. Article 8. The duties of the investigation section are as follows: A. Investigating the general situation and number of civilian boatmen in this city, B. Investigating the general situation of past organizations of workers in this industry in this city, C. Other investigation matters. Article 9. The duties of the guidance section are as follows: A. Guiding the organization of workers of this party, B. Guiding the activities of workers in this industry, C. Guiding and supervising various election matters, D. Other guidance matters. Article 10. The Reorganization Committee may, depending on the complexity of the affairs, discretionarily set up one to three staff members, and those who are qualified as secretaries of the original labor union shall be appointed first. Article 11. The Reorganization Committee shall hold a meeting once a week. When necessary, temporary meetings may be convened. Article 12. Members and instructors of the Reorganization Committee are all voluntary positions, but staff members may be given living expenses. Article 13. The reorganization period of the Reorganization Committee is set at three months. Second article, the Reorganization Committee will be replaced by the official establishment of the Shanghai Civilian Boatmen's Union at the time of the East. Article 15. The detailed rules for the Reorganization Committee's office shall be determined separately. Article 16. These rules shall be deliberated and promulgated by the Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang.
